For more information about what you can do with this app, check https://www.kali.org/kali-on-windows-app.\r\n\r\nNote: Some tools may trigger Antivirus warnings when installed, please plan ahead accordingly. Make sure to visit our Kali on WSL tutorial page at https://www.kali.org/news/kali-linux-in-the-windows-app-store\r\n\r\nBe sure to enable the Windows Subsystem for Linux optional feature before installing the Kali Linux app!","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Most popular","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;mostPopular;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":996,"PageSize":200}}
